    customer_name STRING,
    email STRING,
    address STRING
);


CREATE TABLE reviews (
    review_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    product_id UUID,
    customer_id UUID,
    rating INT,
    review_text TEXT
);


CREATE TABLE orders (
    order_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    customer_id UUID,
    product_id UUID,
    quantity INT,
    order_date DATE
);


CREATE TABLE categories (
    category_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    category_name STRING
);
